Natalie will be a PhD researcher at Aarhus University's Department of Culture and Society, working on an interdisciplinary project that brings together biology and anthropology to consider human altered landscapes (see http://anthropocene.au.dk/). Graeme is a software and web-developer and will be looking for contract or full-time work with technology start-ups in Aarhus. We are avid cyclists and enjoy the outdoors (camping, swimming, hiking, sailing, kayaking, skiing, etc.). We are excited to immerse ourselves in Danish life and culture, and are looking to live in an interesting and central neighborhood, for a furnished or unfurnished apartment, one or two bedrooms, somewhere in the range of 12 000 DKK per month.

These tests are in preparation for my Danish citizenship exam, i am taking with all the other hopeful foreigners, on November 30, 2017.  I have to get 34 out of 40 correct.  To be honest, I have never been so unsure of whether I will pass or not.  No. I will pass!!!  Why am I doing this?  Because I feel like a Dane and want to be able to vote at the government elections in the country I have spent two- thirds of my life:). I have not been able to vote in canada while I live here.   And also because it is now possible to become a danish citizen AND keep my Canadian citizenship. I have been here for forty-two years and have been waiting for this possibility.   I must say that if I knew that I had to study so much to start getting even average results, that I would never have started.   Now I have begun, have paid almost 400 dollars, used many hours studying, well, of course I will finish it.   These are links to the tests that I have been taking daily. A company has made an online studying forum, and one of their products is these daily test, to drill us through the 178 page book.

In support of mental illness. Maybe if people's heads weren't buried in the sand of ignorance and they took the time to understand, instead of judging and thinking it won't happen to them because they have the perfect family, life would be a little bit easier for people that do experience this! This hits close to home for me, for family and friends who live under this shadow. The days of 'it' not being talked about or being taboo should be over. In the most difficult moments of life you realize who your true friends are, and the people who really appreciate you. Unfortunately, most social media 'friends' aren't true friends. They will send you a "like" here and there, but in reality they do not take time to read your status if they see it's lengthy. More than half will stop reading right here, or have already scrolled on to the next post on their page. I decided to post this message in support of all those who continue to battle with their mental illness. Now, let's see who will have taken the time to read this lengthy post right through to the end. If you have read everything so far, please "like" it so that I can put a thank you on your page. More mental health awareness is urgently needed. Just because you can't see it, doesn't mean people aren't suffering. Please, try to spare a little of your time with someone who may just want to talk (about anything). Talking can help us all to cope a little more, keeping things bottled up just makes it worse. Most people will say, "if you need anything, don't hesitate to call me, I'll be there to help you" but will they? I believe a select few of my friends will post this, to show their support for those who may be struggling. You just have to copy and paste rather than sharing. I'd like to know who will take a minute out of their day to read this all the way to the end and then copy and paste it to their page, will you? If so, please write "done" in the comments.

1500 mink farms in Denmark have been ordered to slaughter all of their mink, because of the mutant COVID 19 - cluster 5. It is not reacting to the antidrugs in the same way that the COVID 19 does, meaning it will be resistant to the new vaccines.   These farms  produce approximately 17 million mink skins every year. The largest mink producent country in the world.   They will close all production of minks, probably for the coming many years.300 thousand people will be restricted, schools, public transportation will close.   So sad for so many people.  People who have worked to make the best mink in the world, and have done so for generations.   So good that the danish government is taking this new situation very seriously.  Whatever one thinks about minks- doesnât matter. There are so many people whose lives are drastically changed  by this.
